\subsection{Detailed Description}
Defines keyboard scancodes. 

\subsection{Enumeration Type Documentation}
\index{S\+D\+L\+\_\+scancode.\+h@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+scancode.\+h}!S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+Scancode@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+Scancode}}
\index{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+Scancode@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+Scancode}!S\+D\+L\+\_\+scancode.\+h@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+scancode.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{\texorpdfstring{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+Scancode}{SDL_Scancode}}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}enum {\bf S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+Scancode}}\hypertarget{_s_d_l__scancode_8h_a82ab7cff701034fb40a47b5b3a02777b}{}\label{_s_d_l__scancode_8h_a82ab7cff701034fb40a47b5b3a02777b}


The S\+DL keyboard scancode representation. 

Values of this type are used to represent keyboard keys, among other places in the \hyperlink{struct_s_d_l___keysym_ad47e9120a511e2efc7ec0c6d8a5ec51e}{key.\+keysym.\+scancode } field of the \hyperlink{union_s_d_l___event}{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+Event} structure.

The values in this enumeration are based on the U\+SB usage page standard\+: \href{http://www.usb.org/developers/devclass_docs/Hut1_12v2.pdf}{\tt http\+://www.\+usb.\+org/developers/devclass\+\_\+docs/\+Hut1\+\_\+12v2.\+pdf} \begin{Desc}
